78 window.__bufferedErrors.push({

79 message: message,

80 url: url,

81 line: line,

82 column: column,

83 error: error

84 });

85 return false;

87 window.__initialData = {

88 pending: true,

89 waiting: []

90 };

91 function asyncFetchSharedData(extra) {

92 var sharedDataReq = new XMLHttpRequest();

93 sharedDataReq.onreadystatechange = function() {

94 if (sharedDataReq.readyState === 4) {

95 if(sharedDataReq.status === 200){

96 var sharedData = JSON.parse(sharedDataReq.responseText);

97 window.__initialDataLoaded(sharedData, extra);

98 }

99 }

100 }

101 sharedDataReq.open('GET', '/data/shared_data/', true);

102 sharedDataReq.send(null);

103 }

104 function notifyLoaded(item, data) {

105 item.pending = false;

106 item.data = data;

107 for (var i = 0;i < item.waiting.length; ++i) {

108 item.waiting[i].resolve(item.data);

109 }

110 item.waiting = [];

111 }

112 function notifyError(item, msg) {

113 item.pending = false;

114 item.error = new Error(msg);

115 for (var i = 0;i < item.waiting.length; ++i) {

116 item.waiting[i].reject(item.error);

117 }

118 item.waiting = [];

119 }

120 window.__initialDataLoaded = function(initialData, extraData) {

121 if (extraData) {

122 for (var key in extraData) {

123 initialData[key] = extraData[key];

124 }

125 }

126 notifyLoaded(window.__initialData, initialData);

127 };

128 window.__initialDataError = function(msg) {

129 notifyError(window.__initialData, msg);

130 };

131 window.__additionalData = {};

132 window.__pendingAdditionalData = function(paths) {

133 for (var i = 0;i < paths.length; ++i) {

134 window.__additionalData[paths[i]] = {

135 pending: true,

136 waiting: []

137 };

138 }

139 };

140 window.__additionalDataLoaded = function(path, data) {

141 if (path in window.__additionalData) {

142 notifyLoaded(window.__additionalData[path], data);

143 } else {

144 console.error('Unexpected additional data loaded "' + path + '"');

145 }

146 };

147 window.__additionalDataError = function(path, msg) {

148 if (path in window.__additionalData) {

149 notifyError(window.__additionalData[path], msg);

150 } else {

151 console.error('Unexpected additional data encountered an error "' + path + '": ' + msg);

152 }

153 };

154

155})();
